The design allows to declare some cores as \"dummy\". It was found practical to try 10-20 cores each Map and Place & Route run while the rest of the cores are declared as dummy ones. After such a run, Post Place and Route Static Timing Report is used to find which cores don't violate timing. That cores are marked as \"good\", declared as \"dummy\" for the next run, result files containing \"good\" placement are saved into a separate \"export\" directory. Typically up to 50% cores in a run are OK, while some cores continue to violate timing after many attempts. In such a case FPGA editor is used to see what's wrong and to make design decisions such as to review area constraints.
